<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:66.66%">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Hi, I&#8217;m Elle</strong>!</h2>



<p>I’m Elle Reed, a passionate veggie gardener who believes that anyone can grow their own food, no matter their space or experience. I’ve grown vegetables in a small central London apartment and now, as a mum, in a small urban backyard. Through these experiences, I’ve learned that space doesn’t have to limit your gardening dreams. </p>



<p>Like anything new, it helps to have a community – that&#8217;s why I&#8217;ve created this blog. Let’s start this edible journey together – because we <strong>can all grow our own food, wherever we are!</strong></p>
</div>
</div>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-sitka-classic-light-accent-background-color has-background">How to Start a Vegetable Garden in Your Backyard</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Starting a vegetable garden in your backyard is a rewarding way to enjoy fresh, homegrown produce. When I first started gardening in my urban backyard, I was amazed at how quickly a small space could yield so much, and how much the kids loved getting involved. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Whether you&#8217;re new to gardening or seeking vegetable gardening tips for beginners, these four articles are where I recommend you start. They cover everything from how to start a vegetable garden to essential techniques for vegetable gardening for beginners. Dive in and discover how simple and satisfying growing your own vegetables can be!</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-sitka-classic-light-accent-background-color has-background">How to Grow Vegetables in an Apartment</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Growing vegetables in an apartment is not only possible but incredibly rewarding. Whether you have a balcony or not, indoor vegetable gardening is possible and can provide you with fresh produce right at home. When I lived in London, I had just a small balcony, but I quickly proved that it was possible to grow vegetables in small spaces! </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">The four articles below are where I recommend you start. They’ll guide you through the essentials of indoor vegetable gardening and gardening in an apartment, helping you maximize your space and start growing fresh, healthy food today!</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-sitka-classic-light-accent-background-color has-background">How to Compost at Home for Beginners</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Composting at home is a fantastic way to reduce waste and create nutrient-rich soil for your garden. When I first began composting, I was surprised at how easy it was to turn kitchen scraps and yard waste into something so beneficial for my plants. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">If you’re new to composting and wondering how to compost effectively, the articles below are where I recommend you start. They cover everything from the basics of composting for beginners to detailed tips on how to compost at home, even in small spaces. Dive in and discover how rewarding and straightforward composting at home can be!</p>

<p></p>
<cite><strong>What is a Potager?<br></strong><em>A "potager" (pn. pot-a-jer) is a French kitchen garden that's close enough to the kitchen to be accessible all year round, whilst being viewed as a thing of beauty!</em></cite></blockquote>
</div><div id="sitka_about_widget-1" class="widget sitka_about_widget"><h4 class="widget-title">About Me</h4>

								<h5 class="about-name">Elle Reed</h5>
								
								<span class="about-label">Gardener &amp; Blogger</span>
								
								<p>I'm a firm believer that anyone can grow vegetables; the key is to start somewhere! Whether it’s a few herb pots, a potager, or a full garden plot, let's embark on this journey towards growing our own food together. </p>

data-wpel-link="external">
			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Stop throwing out onion skins 🧅 You can turn them </span>
						<svg style="color: rgba(255,255,255,1)" class="svg-inline--fa fa-play fa-w-14 sbi_playbtn" aria-label="Play" aria-hidden="true" data-fa-processed="" data-prefix="fa" data-icon="play" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M424.4 214.7L72.4 6.6C43.8-10.3 0 6.1 0 47.9V464c0 37.5 40.7 60.1 72.4 41.3l352-208c31.4-18.5 31.5-64.1 0-82.6z"></path></svg>			<img width="1000" height="560" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201000%20560'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Stop throwing out onion skins 🧅 You can turn them into homemade onion powder!

I keep adding skins to a bag in the freezer until I have enough. Then I dehydrate them (around 60–70°C in the oven or dehydrator) until completely dry.

Blend them up… and that’s it.

The smell is incredible and it’s such a simple way to use the whole onion and reduce waste.

I only do this with organic onions or ones from my garden (red or brown it doesn&#039;t matter) since you’re using the skins.

Did you know you could do this? 💚

I keep adding skins to a bag in the freezer until I have enough. Then I dehydrate them (around 60–70°C in the oven or dehydrator) until completely dry.

Blend them up… and that’s it.

The smell is incredible and it’s such a simple way to use the whole onion and reduce waste.

I only do this with organic onions or ones from my garden (red or brown it doesn&#039;t matter) since you’re using the skins.

Did you know you could do this? 💚

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">The true cost of eating well has got to be time!

</span>
						<svg style="color: rgba(255,255,255,1)" class="svg-inline--fa fa-play fa-w-14 sbi_playbtn" aria-label="Play" aria-hidden="true" data-fa-processed="" data-prefix="fa" data-icon="play" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M424.4 214.7L72.4 6.6C43.8-10.3 0 6.1 0 47.9V464c0 37.5 40.7 60.1 72.4 41.3l352-208c31.4-18.5 31.5-64.1 0-82.6z"></path></svg>			<img width="1000" height="560" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201000%20560'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="The true cost of eating well has got to be time!

Some days I honestly feel like throwing my hands up and saying, “Let’s just buy it from the supermarket!”

Sourdough needs feeding.
Veggies need picking, washing, and storing.
Eggs need collecting.
And homemade baking definitely isn’t instant.

When you’re a working mum, time is often the one thing you don’t have much of. I completely understand how convenience food became so popular. Life is busy.
But when I look at my family… and remind myself of my why — reducing additives, avoiding unnecessary toxins, and nourishing our bodies with real food — it helps me keep showing up.

And honestly… it just tastes better too 😉

If you’re trying to grow, cook, or make more from scratch, remember you don’t have to do everything at once. Just start somewhere 💚

Some days I honestly feel like throwing my hands up and saying, “Let’s just buy it from the supermarket!”

Sourdough needs feeding.
Veggies need picking, washing, and storing.
Eggs need collecting.
And homemade baking definitely isn’t instant.

When you’re a working mum, time is often the one thing you don’t have much of. I completely understand how convenience food became so popular. Life is busy.
But when I look at my family… and remind myself of my why — reducing additives, avoiding unnecessary toxins, and nourishing our bodies with real food — it helps me keep showing up.

And honestly… it just tastes better too 😉

If you’re trying to grow, cook, or make more from scratch, remember you don’t have to do everything at once. Just start somewhere 💚

data-wpel-link="external">
			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Don&#039;t get me wrong, I love summer days 🌞, but afte</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201000%20560'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Don&#039;t get me wrong, I love summer days 🌞, but after a week of hot sun, nothing makes my gardener heart happier than a good downpour! 🤗🌧
.
Anyone else with me?

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">When life gives you an abundance of strawberries… </span>
						<svg style="color: rgba(255,255,255,1)" class="svg-inline--fa fa-play fa-w-14 sbi_playbtn" aria-label="Play" aria-hidden="true" data-fa-processed="" data-prefix="fa" data-icon="play" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M424.4 214.7L72.4 6.6C43.8-10.3 0 6.1 0 47.9V464c0 37.5 40.7 60.1 72.4 41.3l352-208c31.4-18.5 31.5-64.1 0-82.6z"></path></svg>			<img width="1000" height="560" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201000%20560'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="When life gives you an abundance of strawberries… you make jam. 🍓✨

There’s something so satisfying about turning a bucket of fresh, ripe berries into jars of sweet, glossy strawberry jam that you can enjoy long after the season is over.

Here’s my simple small-batch strawberry jam:

🍓 Ingredients
• 1 kg strawberries, hulled
• 750 g sugar
• Juice of 1 lemon

Method

Chop the strawberries and place them in a large pot with the sugar and lemon juice.

Bring to a gentle boil, stirring to dissolve the sugar.

Simmer for 20–30 minutes, stirring often, until thick and glossy.

Test for set (a little on a cold plate should wrinkle when pushed).

Pour into hot, sterilised jars and seal.

And just like that… summer in a jar 💛

If you’d love to learn how to preserve with confidence — not just jams, but fruit, veg, meals and more — come join us inside our online Jar By Jar Preserving Course.

👉 Learn more at jarbyjar.com

Because once you know how to preserve… you’ll never look at a full fruit bowl the same way again. 🍓✨

<script>class RocketElementorAnimation{constructor(){this.deviceMode=document.createElement("span"),this.deviceMode.id="elementor-device-mode",this.deviceMode.setAttribute("class","elementor-screen-only"),document.body.appendChild(this.deviceMode)}_detectAnimations(){let t=getComputedStyle(this.deviceMode,":after").content.replace(/"/g,"");this.animationSettingKeys=this._listAnimationSettingsKeys(t),document.querySelectorAll(".elementor-invisible[data-settings]").forEach(t=>{const e=t.getBoundingClientRect();if(e.bottom>=0&&e.top<=window.innerHeight)try{this._animateElement(t)}catch(t){}})}_animateElement(t){const e=JSON.parse(t.dataset.settings),i=e._animation_delay||e.animation_delay||0,n=e[this.animationSettingKeys.find(t=>e[t])];if("none"===n)return void t.classList.remove("elementor-invisible");t.classList.remove(n),this.currentAnimation&&t.classList.remove(this.currentAnimation),this.currentAnimation=n;let s=setTimeout(()=>{t.classList.remove("elementor-invisible"),t.classList.add("animated",n),this._removeAnimationSettings(t,e)},i);window.addEventListener("rocket-startLoading",function(){clearTimeout(s)})}_listAnimationSettingsKeys(t="mobile"){const e=[""];switch(t){case"mobile":e.unshift("_mobile");case"tablet":e.unshift("_tablet");case"desktop":e.unshift("_desktop")}const i=[];return["animation","_animation"].forEach(t=>{e.forEach(e=>{i.push(t+e)})}),i}_removeAnimationSettings(t,e){this._listAnimationSettingsKeys().forEach(t=>delete e[t]),t.dataset.settings=JSON.stringify(e)}static run(){const t=new RocketElementorAnimation;requestAnimationFrame(t._detectAnimations.bind(t))}}document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",RocketElementorAnimation.run);</script></body>
